***marinier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a> (7213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in the mid 17th century. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mariniers.html>mariniers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>mariniertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>marine</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The literal translation of "<a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>marine</i>. However, a Dutch "<a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on a par with a US Navy SEAL. A US Marine <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> somewhat equivalent to a Dutch Landmacht <a href = vnd.unilang:soldaat.html>soldaat</a>.</li></ul>
<hr />

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">market</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">marct</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*markat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marcātus</i>, an alternative form of Classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mercātus</i>.

***marlin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a> (16516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">marlinspike</i>, named so because of its pointed snout.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">marlins</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any species of game fish belonging to either of the genera <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tetrapturus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tetrapturus"><i>Tetrapturus</i></a></span> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Makaira" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Makaira"><i>Makaira</i></a></span>. Every such species <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a pointed, spear-like projection of the upper jaw.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spearfish</span></li></ul>
</body>

***marmer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marmer.html>marmer</a> (15044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:marmer.html>marmer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marmor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μάρμαρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mármaros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marmer.html>marmer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)

***maroon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> (60134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feral; fugitive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cimarrón</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fugitive, wild, feral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(people)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (people)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> (people)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(people)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (people)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An escaped negro slave of the Caribbean and the Americas or a descendant of escaped slaves. <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1985</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wade_Davis_(anthropologist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wade Davis (anthropologist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:wade.html>Wade</a> Davis</a>, <i>The Serpent and the Rainbow</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> amp; Schuster, p. 193:
<dl><dd>Further north a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a></b> community in the Bahoruco Mountains thrived for eighty-five years, until the French proposed a truce under the <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of which the <b>Maroons</b> would be permitted to form an independent clan.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, Kevin Filan, <i>The Haitian Vodou Handbook</i>, Destiny Books 2007, p. 14:
<dl><dd>Joining others who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> escaped before them, they formed communities of <b>Maroons</b> in which many traditional African customs and social mores <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> preserved.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A castaway; a person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> marooned. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">castaway</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Associated with <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> culture, communities or peoples.
<ul><li><b>2002</b>, Cynthia James, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> Narrative: Caribbean Literature in English Across Boundaries, Ethnicities, and Centuries</i>, Heinemann Educational Books
<dl><dd>In her discussion of Michelle <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a>'s <i>Abeng</i>, a novel that historicizes <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> culture and the Jamaican warrior heroine Nanny of the Maroons, Francoise Lionnet examines linguistic “metissage” <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">marooning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">marooned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To abandon in a remote, desolate place, as on a desert island.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Brogan Steele, <i>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:jaws.html>Jaws</a> of Death: Extreme True Adventures of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. Nature</i>, St. Martin's <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>Griffin</a> (→ISBN), page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=pRQsO5OVLTcCamp;lpg=PA231amp;dq=%22marooned%22amp;hl=deamp;pg=PA231v=onepage">231</a>:
<dl><dd>After the harrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>stories</a> of being <b>marooned</b> at sea and stranded in the frozen wastelands of Alaska and the <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>Poles</a>, one would think that survival on dry <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> would be easier <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chestnut; brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">marrone</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chestnut; brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μάραον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">máraon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweet chestnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare Spanish <span class="Latn" lang="es">marrón</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(color)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (color)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> (color)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(color)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (color)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A rich dark red, somewhat brownish, color.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> colour: <span style="background-color:800000; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Long, <i>The Nikon D90 Companion: Practical Photography Advice You Can Take Anywhere</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Reilly Media, Inc. (→ISBN), page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=3ukYp2HE9KQCamp;lpg=PA176amp;dq=%22a%20maroon%22amp;hl=deamp;pg=PA176v=onepage">176</a>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> it a really dark <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> or a lighter <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> or a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> that leans toward the red side? Or the <a href = vnd.unilang:magenta.html>magenta</a> side? To address this issue, scientists use something called a color space.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> color</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Possibly owing to the fact that the color of a fired flare <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> commonly red.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/maroon_(rocket)" class="extiw" title="w:maroon (rocket)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> (rocket)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/maroon_(rocket)" class="extiw" title="w:maroon (rocket)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rocket-propelled firework or skyrocket, often one used as a signal (e.g. to summon the crew of a lifeboat or warn of an air raid).
<ul><li><b>1887</b>, “Metropolitan Reports,” <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chemist_%2B_Druggist" class="extiw" title="w:Chemist + Druggist">The Chemist and Druggist</a></i>, 5 November, 1887, p. 564,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/b19974760M0437">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>On Sunday afternoon a serious firework explosion occurred in Lambeth, whereby three persons <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> seriously injured. Two lads <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> purchased a firework called a “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>”, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a bomb consisting of a small ball of string covered with a red composition. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> loaded with gunpowder, and there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also a fuse attached.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1891</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Archer_(critic)" class="extiw" title="w:William Archer (critic)">William <a href = vnd.unilang:archer.html>Archer</a></a> (translator), “At the Fair” in <i>Tales of Two Countries</i> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Kielland" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Kielland">Alexander Kielland</a>, New York: Harper, p. 73,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/talesoftwocountr00kieliala">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>As the evening falls, colored lamps and Chinese lanterns are lighted around the venerable oak which <a href = vnd.unilang:stands.html>stands</a> in the middle of the fairground and boys climb about among its topmost <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a> with <b>maroons</b> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bengal_light" class="extiw" title="w:Bengal light">Bengal lights</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1900</b>, Alan C. Jenkins, <i>Introducing <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>Horses</a></i>, London: Spring Books,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/introducinghorse00jenk">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Many a seaman’s life may have depended on equine speed and strength. Some of these ‘Lifeboat <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>Horses</a>’ used to recognise the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fired to summon the Lifeboat crew. Long after its retirement one of the <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a> which regularly helped to haul the Hoylake Lifeboat <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> fired one day when it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> working in the neighbouring fields. It immediately became very excited and made for the boathouse.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1932</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Bernard_Shaw" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Bernard Shaw">George <a href = vnd.unilang:bernard.html>Bernard</a> Shaw</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Too_True_to_Be_Good" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Too True to Be Good">Too True to Be Good</a></i>, Act II,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks03/0300591h.html">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>And now I am off to inspect stores. There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a shortage of <b>maroons</b> that I don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> understand.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1933</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._G._Wells" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H. G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Shape_of_Things_to_Come" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Shape of Things to Come">The Shape of <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>Things</a> to Come</a></i>, Book 2, Chapter 9,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.net.au/ebooks03/0301391h.html">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The big air <a href = vnd.unilang:raids.html>raids</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> much more dreadful than the air <a href = vnd.unilang:raids.html>raids</a> of the World War. They began with a nightmare of warning <b>maroons</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sirens.html>sirens</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hooters.html>hooters</a> and the shrill whistles of cyclist <a href = vnd.unilang:scouts.html>scouts</a>, then swarms of frantic people running to and fro <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an intentional mispronunciation of the word <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moron</i> used by the cartoon character <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bugs_Bunny" class="extiw" title="w:Bugs Bunny"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugs.html>Bugs</a> Bunny</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An idiot; a fool.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">fool</span>, Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, S. Watts <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a>, <i>Tarnish</i>, IUniverse (2011), →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=jqn8HMZTeRICamp;pg=PA21">page 21</a>:
<dl><dd>At least, I would not be sleeping that night. Why <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> I have that espresso? What a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***marr.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marr.html>marr</a> (46955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marhaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mearh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">mar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">marah</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌰𐍂𐌷𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">marhs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:marr.html>marr</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>horse</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mari.html>mari</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*móri</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mere</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mere</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">mere</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">mar</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">meri</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>Meer</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">meri</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>Meer</a></i>).
</p>

***marshmallow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a> (26586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mersċmealwe</i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">marsh</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mallow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallows.html>marshmallows</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A species of mallow, <i>Althaea officinalis</i>, that grows in marshy terrain. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1653</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicholas_Culpeper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nicholas Culpeper">Nicholas Culpeper</a>, <i>The English Physician Enlarged</i>, Folio Society 2007, page 180:
<dl><dd>Our common <b>Marsh Mallows</b> have diverse soft, hoary white stalks <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> to be three or four foot high, spreading forth many <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A type of confectionery, originally (since Ancient Egyptian times) made from this plant, but now generally made of sugar or corn syrup, gelatin that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> pre-softened in water, gum arabic, flavorings, and sometimes beaten egg whites, all whipped to a spongy consistency. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span> <i>Love, Life and Work</i>:
<dl><dd>The Disagreeable Girl <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a female of the genus <a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a> persuasion, built around a digestive apparatus that possesses marked <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> proclivities.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span> PH Wodehouse, <i>A Wodehouse Miscellany</i>:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an apple <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:sundae.html>sundae</a>, I recollect. I dug my spoon into it with an assumption of gaiety which I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> far from feeling.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> soft and benign.
<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> like a total badass, but he's really just a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b> once you get to know him.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b>  <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:sponzig.html>sponzig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snoepje.html>snoepje</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:volgens.html>Volgens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ulf.html>Ulf</a> Schott, <a href = vnd.unilang:verantwoordelijk.html>verantwoordelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> jeugdbeleid <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duitse.html>Duitse</a> voetbalbond, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> jeugdvoetbal <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:marshmallow.html>marshmallow</a></b>-experiment’ <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitstel.html>uitstel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> behoeftebevrediging. „Kinderen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> offers <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdeling.html>verdeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:disciplineren.html>gedisciplineerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:presteren.html>presteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zowel.html>zowel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> school <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> in sport.” <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***martelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a> (10272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>This word seems to come from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
However, it originates from latin <i>Martyr</i>. Between 1201 and 1250 the word <i>martelare</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in use in Dutch, and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from this word.
The '<a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a>' -aar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not really the common <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a>, but an elongation or derivation of the Latin word.
Therefore, a <a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not someone who tortures (<a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a>), but an actual martyr, who undergoes the torture (<a href = vnd.unilang:gemarteld.html>gemarteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaars.html>martelaars</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaren.html>martelaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelaar.html>martelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>martyr</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijdt.html>lijdt</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:sterft.html>sterft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:symbool.html>symbool</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strijd.html>strijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemarteld.html>gemarteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:martelares.html>martelares</a> (68835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:martelen.html>martelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ares</i>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:marter.html>marter</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">martre</i>, in turn borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*marthar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marþraz</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>To (give a) massage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To work on, prepare, position etc.; notably in billiards, give a head-shot with side-effect</li></ol>

***mastiff.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a> (81558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mastif</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mastyf</i>, an aberrant derivation (with influence from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mestif</i>) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mastin</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mâtin</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*mansuetinus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tamed (animal)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mansuetus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tamed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mastiffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One of an old breed of powerful, deep-chested, and smooth-coated dogs, used chiefly as watchdogs and guard dogs.
<ul><li><b>1605</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear">King Lear</a></i>, Act III, Scene VI
<dl><dd>Avaunt, you curs! Be thy mouth or black or white, Tooth that poisons if it bite; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>Mastiff</a></b>, greyhound, mongrel grim, Hound or <a href = vnd.unilang:spaniel.html>spaniel</a>, brach or him.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1896</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" class="extiw" title="w:Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ranch.html>Ranch</a> Life and the Hunting-Trail</i>, The Century Co., chapter 11
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>Mastiff</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a good fighter, and can kill a wildcat, taking the necessary punishment well, as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> found out when <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> once trapped one of these small lynxes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodont.html>mastodont</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodonten.html>mastodonten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mastodont.html>mastodontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mastodon</span>, mammal of the family Mammutidae, especially of the genus <i>Mammut</i> <span class="defdate">[from 1807]</span>
<ul><li><b>1807</b> April 3, "<a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschappen.html>Wetenschappen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:letteren.html>letteren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunsten.html>kunsten</a>", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:koninklijke.html>Koninklijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>courant</a></i>, issue 80, page 3.

***mat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> mat (7015)</h1><br></body> 
***matador.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a> (29813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">killer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Used in the English language as title for a bullfighter, however referred to as a <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">torero</i> in Spain.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matadors.html>matadors</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:matadores.html>matadores</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">matadora</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">bullfighting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The person whose aim <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to kill the bull in a bullfight.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A certain game of dominoes in which four dominoes (the 4-3, 5-2, 6-1, and double <a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a>), called <i><a href = vnd.unilang:matadors.html>matadors</a></i>, may be played at any time in any way.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:clubs.html>clubs</a>, or any other trump <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in sequence with it, in the game of <a href = vnd.unilang:skat.html>skat</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the three chief cards in ombre and <a href = vnd.unilang:quadrille.html>quadrille</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:matador.html>matador</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:stierenvechter.html>stierenvechter</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> eersten</li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>[1] espada, toreador, torero</li></ul>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>[1] banderillero, picador</li></ul>
